&DOFXODWLRQ URXWLQHV
&
,QWHUSRODWLRQ URXWLQH IRU WKH &23PDS
1
def get_COP_map(Load, T_SR_in , T_DH_forward , df_COP_map):
2
""" calculates the COP depending on df_COP_map (excel), based on load
3
4
Parameters
5
----------
6
Load: float
7
load of the hp (0%-100%)
8
T_SR_in: float
9
source temperature in
10
T_DH_forward: float
11
sink temperature out
12
df_COP_map: DataFrame
13
COP map from the SVAF hp model (paper, Jørgensen)
14
15
Returns
16
-------
17
COP: float
18
COP
19
T_SR_out: float
20
outgoing heat source temperature
21
"""
22
23
# Load
24
if Load < 80:
25
Load_l = 60 # l = low
26
Load_u = 80 # u = up
27
else:
28
Load_l = 80
29
Load_u = 100
30
31
# calculating lower and upper COP for load interpolation
32
COP_l, T_SR_out_l = get_df_T(Load_l, T_SR_in , T_DH_forward , df_COP_map)
33
COP_u, T_SR_out_u = get_df_T(Load_u, T_SR_in , T_DH_forward , df_COP_map)
34
35
# final interpolation based on load
36
COP = get_interpolation(COP_l, COP_u, Load_l, Load_u, Load)
37
T_SR_out = get_interpolation(T_SR_out_l , T_SR_out_u , Load_l, Load_u, Load)
38
39
return COP, T_SR_out
40
41
def get_interpolation(f0, f1, x0, x1, x):
42
# simple interpolation
43
f = f0 +(f1-f0)*(x-x0)/(x1-x0)
44
return f

def get_df_T(Load, T_SR_in , T_DH_forward , df_COP_map):

""" interpolates the COP depending on df_COP_map (excel), based on T sink
3

5DPSLQJ
1
R = dict_settings_par['H']['HP-R-up'] # kW/min, same ramp-up and down
limit
2
for t in range(1,len(df_schedule_da)):
3
delta_flow = df_schedule_da['HP'][t] - df_schedule_da['HP'][t-1] # kW
4
5
# up delta_flow = 0
6
if delta_flow == 0:
7
df_schedule_da_out['HP'][t] = df_schedule_da['HP'][t]
8
9
# up delta_flow > 0
10
elif delta_flow > 0:
11
R_time_min = delta_flow/R
12
13
# no ramping limit constraint
14
if R_time_min < 1:
15
df_schedule_da_out['HP'][t] = df_schedule_da['HP'][t]
16
else:
17
R_time = 60*R_time_min # min*60 = sec time
18
R_part = R_time/tb # [-]
19
20
R_t_int = int(R_time_min)
21
R_t_rest = R_time_min - R_t_int
22
R_full = sum(range(R_t_int+1))
23
24
# kWh =
1h * part * kW = kWh
+ part 1h * kWmin / 60min = kWh
25
E_kWh = (1-R_part)*delta_flow + R_part*(R*R_full + R*R_t_rest)
/60
26
df_schedule_da_out['HP'][t] = df_schedule_da['HP'][t-1] +
E_kWh
27
28
# dw delta_flow < 0
29
elif delta_flow < 0:
30
R_time_min = abs(delta_flow)/R
31
32
# no ramping limit constraint
33
if R_time_min < 1:
34
df_schedule_da_out['HP'][t] = df_schedule_da['HP'][t]
35
else:
36
R_time = 60*R_time_min # min*60 = sec time
37
R_part = R_time/tb # [-]
38
39
R_t_int = int(R_time_min)
40
R_t_rest = R_time_min - R_t_int
41
R_full = sum(range(R_t_int+1))
42
43
# kWh =
1h * part * kW = kWh
+ part 1h * kWmin / 60min = kWh
44
E_kWh = (1-R_part)*abs(delta_flow) + R_part*(R*R_full + R*
R_t_rest)/60
45
df_schedule_da_out['HP'][t] = df_schedule_da['HP'][t-1] -
E_kWh
46
47
df_h_sch = pd.concat([df_schedule_da['HP'], df_schedule_da_out['HP']],
axis=1)
48
df_h_sch.columns =['schedule', 'ramp']
